<time class="updated" datetime="2021-05-13T21:59:06-07:00" style="">May 13, 2021</time>\n<h2 class="content-title"><a href="https://www.organicfacts.net/health-benefits/fruit/pomelo-clone.html">Pomelos: Benefits &amp; How To Eat Them (Pummelo)</a></h2>\n</div>\n<div class="col-lg">\n<div class="content-excerpt-parent primary-multiline-ellipsis"><p>When it comes to pomelos, picking the right fruit can be quite tricky as it can be dramatically different from one to the next whether in terms of color, juiciness, taste, and so on. They can go from being seedless to fruit with too many seeds, yellow to pink, and juicy to absolutely bone dry. However, when compared to their citric counterpart grapefruit, pomelos are less tart and tangy. Notwithstanding their diverse range of flavors, pomelos have several health benefits. However, when compared to their citric counterpart grapefruit, pomelos are less tart and tangy. Notwithstanding their diverse range of flavors, pomelos have several health benefits. For those willing</p></div>\n<a class="content-post-read-more d-inline-block my-2" href="https://www.organicfacts.net/health-benefits/fruit/pomelo-clone.html">READ MORE</a>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</article>\n</div>\n</div><div class="row no-gutters">\n<div class="col-md-4">\n<article class="content-post post-191680 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail category-weight-loss category-fitness category-herbs-and-spices tag-curcumin tag-turmeric-for-weight-loss tag-turmeric-milk tag-turmeric-for-weight">\n<div class="content-body">\n<div class="row">\n<div class="col-6 col-md-12 content-post-secondary">\n<a href="https://www.organicfacts.net/turmeric-weight-loss.html" class="post-thumbnail" aria-hidden="true"><img width="320" height="180" data-src="https://www.organicfacts.net/wp-content/uploads/goldenturmericmilk-320x180.jpg" class="attachment-md-crop size-md-crop wp-post-image" alt="Healthy vegan turmeric latte or golden milk with honey in female hands" data-srcset="https://www.organicfacts.net/wp-content/uploads/goldenturmericmilk-320x180.jpg 320w, https://www.organicfacts.net/wp-content/uploads/goldenturmericmilk-480x270.jpg 480w" sizes="(max-width: 320px) 100vw, 320px" />\n</a>\n<p class="single-author text-uppercase d-none d-md-block">by <span class="author single-author-name"><b><a href="https://www.organicfacts.net/author/raksha" title="Raksha Hegde">Raksha Hegde</a></b></span> last updated - <time class="updated" datetime="2020-11-08T23:45:20-08:00" style="">November 08, 2020</time>\n<h2 class="content-title"><a href="https://www.organicfacts.net/turmeric-weight-loss.html">Is Turmeric Good For Weight Loss</a></h2>\n</div>\n<div class="col-6 col-md-12">\n<div class="content-excerpt-parent secondary-multiline-ellipsis"><p>Turmeric probably tops the list of the most popular spice to boost overall health and immunity.
